<h1 _ngcontent-smf-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="应用级变量的状态管理"> 应用级变量的状态管理 </h1>

<div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>状态管理模块提供了应用程序的数据存储能力、持久化数据管理能力、UIAbility数据存储能力和应用程序需要的环境状态。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>本模块首批接口从API version 7开始支持，后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p>     </div></div></div>    <p>本文中T和S的含义如下：</p>    <div class="tablenoborder">     <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                   <tbody><tr class="firstRow">        <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>        <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>       </tr><tr>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">T</td>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Class，number，boolean，string和这些类型的数组形式。</td>       </tr>       <tr>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">S</td>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">number，boolean，string。</td>       </tr>           </tbody></table></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="appstorage" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">AppStorage<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="appstorage" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>AppStorage具体UI使用说明，详见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage(应用全局的UI状态存储)</a></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 929px;">     <h3 id="ref12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">ref<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="ref12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static ref&lt;T&gt;(propName: string): AbstractProperty&lt;T&gt; | undefined</p>     <p>如果给定的propName在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中存在，则返回AppStorage中propName对应属性的引用。否则，返回undefined。</p>     <p>与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#link10">link</a>的功能基本一致，但不需要手动释放返回的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#abstractproperty12">AbstractProperty</a>类型的变量。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AppStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#abstractproperty12">AbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</a> | undefined</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">AppStorage中propName对应属性的引用，如果AppStorage中不存在对应的propName，则返回undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-title class_">AppStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setOrCreate</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'PropA'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">47</span>);</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">refToPropA1</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">AbstractProperty</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt; | <span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span> = <span class="hljs-title class_">AppStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">ref</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'PropA'</span>);</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">refToPropA2</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">AbstractProperty</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt; | <span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span> = <span class="hljs-title class_">AppStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">ref</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'PropA'</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// refToPropA2.get() == 47</span></li><li>refToPropA1?.<span class="hljs-title function_">set</span>(<span class="hljs-number">48</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// 同步修改AppStorage: refToPropA1.get() == refToPropA2.get() == 48</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1226px;">     <h3 id="setandref12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setAndRef<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setandref12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static setAndRef&lt;T&gt;(propName: string, defaultValue: T): AbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</p>     <p>与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#ref12">ref</a>接口类似，如果给定的propName在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中存在，则返回AppStorage中propName对应属性的引用。如果不存在，则使用defaultValue在AppStorage中创建和初始化propName对应的属性，并返回其引用。defaultValue须为T类型，可以为null或undefined。</p>     <p>与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#setandlink10">setAndLink</a>的功能基本一致，但不需要手动释放返回的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#abstractproperty12">AbstractProperty</a>类型的变量。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始，AppStorage支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰map类型变量" target="_blank">Map</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰set类型变量" target="_blank">Set</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰date类型变量" target="_blank">Date类型</a>，支持null、undefined以及<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#appstorage支持联合类型" target="_blank">联合类型</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AppStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">defaultValue</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">T</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">当propName在AppStorage中不存在时，使用defaultValue在AppStorage中初始化propName对应属性的值，defaultValue可以为null或undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#abstractproperty12">AbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">AbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;的实例，为AppStorage中propName对应属性的引用。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-title class_">AppStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setOrCreate</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'PropA'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">47</span>);</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">ref1</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">AbstractProperty</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-number">49</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// 用默认值49创建PropB</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">ref2</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">AbstractProperty</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt; = <span class="hljs-title class_">AppStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setAndRef</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'PropA'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">50</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// PropA已存在，值为47</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1017px;">     <h3 id="link10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">link<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="link10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static link&lt;T&gt;(propName: string): SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</p>     <p>与<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中对应的propName建立双向数据绑定。如果给定的propName在AppStorage中存在，返回AppStorage中propName对应属性的双向绑定数据。</p>     <p>双向绑定数据的修改会同步回AppStorage中，AppStorage会将变化同步到所有绑定该propName的数据和自定义组件中。</p>     <p>如果AppStorage中不存在propName，则返回undefined。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AppStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#subscribedabstractproperty">SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回双向绑定的数据，如果AppStorage中不存在对应的propName，则返回undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-title class_">AppStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setOrCreate</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'PropA'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">47</span>);</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">linkToPropA1</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">SubscribedAbstractProperty</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt; = <span class="hljs-title class_">AppStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">link</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'PropA'</span>);</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">linkToPropA2</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">SubscribedAbstractProperty</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt; = <span class="hljs-title class_">AppStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">link</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'PropA'</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// linkToPropA2.get() == 47</span></li><li>linkToPropA1.<span class="hljs-title function_">set</span>(<span class="hljs-number">48</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// 双向同步: linkToPropA1.get() == linkToPropA2.get() == 48</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1202px;">     <h3 id="setandlink10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setAndLink<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setandlink10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static setAndLink&lt;T&gt;(propName: string, defaultValue: T): SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</p>     <p>与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#link10">link</a>接口类似，如果给定的propName在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中存在，则返回该propName对应的属性的双向绑定数据。如果不存在，则使用defaultValue在AppStorage中创建和初始化propName对应的属性，返回其双向绑定数据。defaultValue必须为T类型，从API version 12开始defaultValue可以为null或undefined。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始，AppStorage支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰map类型变量" target="_blank">Map</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰set类型变量" target="_blank">Set</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰date类型变量" target="_blank">Date类型</a>，支持null、undefined以及<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#appstorage支持联合类型" target="_blank">联合类型</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.2" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">prop<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="prop10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static prop&lt;T&gt;(propName: string): SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</p>     <p>与<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中对应的propName建立单向属性绑定。如果给定的propName在AppStorage中存在，则返回与AppStorage中propName对应属性的单向绑定数据。如果AppStorage中不存在propName，则返回undefined。单向绑定数据的修改不会被同步回AppStorage中。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AppStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#subscribedabstractproperty">SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回单向绑定的数据，如果AppStorage中不存在对应的propName，则返回undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div class="hljs-number">1</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// 单向同步：prop1.get()的值为1，prop2.get()的值为47</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1154px;">     <h3 id="setandprop10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setAndProp<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setandprop10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static setAndProp&lt;T&gt;(propName: string, defaultValue: T): SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</p>     <p>与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#prop10">prop</a>接口类似。如果给定的propName在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中存在，则返回该propName对应的属性的单向绑定数据。如果不存在，则使用defaultValue在AppStorage中创建和初始化propName对应的属性，返回其单向绑定数据。defaultValue必须为T类型，从API version 12开始defaultValue可以为null或undefined。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始，AppStorage支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰map类型变量" target="_blank">Map</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰set类型变量" target="_blank">Set</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰date类型变量" target="_blank">Date类型</a>，支持null、undefined以及<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#appstorage支持联合类型" target="_blank">联合类型</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AppStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">defaultValue</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">T</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">当propName在AppStorage中不存在时，使用defaultValue在AppStorage中初始化propName对应属性的值，从API version 12开始，defaultValue可以为null或undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">set<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="set10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static set&lt;T&gt;(propName: string, newValue: T): boolean</p>     <p>在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中设置propName对应属性的值。如果newValue的值和propName对应属性的值相同，即不需要做赋值操作，状态变量不会通知UI刷新propName对应属性的值，从API version 12开始，newValue可以为null或undefined。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始，AppStorage支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰map类型变量" target="_blank">Map</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰set类型变量" target="_blank">Set</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰date类型变量" target="_blank">Date类型</a>，支持null、undefined以及<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#appstorage支持联合类型" target="_blank">联合类型</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table> width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>      <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">T</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">属性值，从API version 12开始可以为null或undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.14.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.14.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">如果AppStorage中不存在propName对应的属性，或设值失败，则返回false。设置成功则返回true。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106=""   <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 887px;">     <h3 id="setorcreate10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setOrCreate<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setorcreate10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static setOrCreate&lt;T&gt;(propName: string, newValue: T): void</p>     <p>如果propName已经在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中存在，并且newValue和propName对应属性的值不同，则设置propName对应属性的值为newValue，否则状态变量不会通知UI刷新propName对应属性的值。</p>     <p>如果propName不存在，则创建propName属性，值为newValue。setOrCreate只可以创建单个AppStorage的键值对，如果想创建多个AppStorage键值对，可以多次调用此方法。从API version 12开始，newValue可以为null或undefined。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始，AppStorage支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰map类型变量" target="_blank">Map</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰set类型变量" target="_blank">Set</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#装饰date类型变量" target="_blank">Date类型</a>，支持null、undefined以及<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#appstorage支持联合类型" target="_blank">联合类型</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.15.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.15.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.15.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.15.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AppStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">newValue</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">T</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">属性值，从API version 12开始可以为null或undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1297px;">     <h3 id="delete10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">delete<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="delete10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static delete(propName: string): boolean</p>     <p>在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中删除propName对应的属性。</p>     <p>在AppStorage中删除该属性的前提是必须保证该属性没有订阅者。如果有订阅者，则返回false。如果没有订阅者，则删除成功并返回true。</p>     <p>属性的订阅者为：</p>     <ol>      <li>       <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#storagelink" target="_blank">@StorageLink</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#storageprop" target="_blank">@StorageProp</a>装饰的变量。</p></li>      <li>       <p>通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#link10">link</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#prop10">prop</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#setandlink10">setAndLink</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#setandprop10">setAndProp</a>接口返回的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#subscribedabstractproperty">SubscribedAbstractProperty</a>的实例。</p></li>     </ol>     <p>如果想要删除这些订阅者，可以通过以下方式：</p>     <ol>      <li>       <p>删除@StorageLink、@StorageProp所在的自定义组件。删除自定义组件请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-page-custom-components-lifecycle#自定义组件的删除" target="_blank">自定义组件的删除</a>。</p></li>      <li>       <p>对link、prop、setAndLink、setAndProp接口返回的SubscribedAbstractProperty的实例调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#abouttobedeleted10">aboutToBeDeleted</a>接口。</p></li>     </ol>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.16.12.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.16.12.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.16.12.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.16.12.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AppStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.16.14.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.16.14.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">如果AppStorage中有对应的属性，且该属性已经没有订阅者，则删除成功，返回true。如果属性不存在，或者该属性还存在订阅者，则返回false。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder"> class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 770px;">     <h3 id="clear10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">clear<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="clear10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static clear(): boolean</p>     <p>删除<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中所有属性。删除所有属性的前提是，AppStorage已经没有任何订阅者。如果有订阅者，clear将不会生效并返回false。如果没有订阅者，则删除成功，并返回true。</p>     <p>订阅者的含义参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#delete10">delete</a>。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.8.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.8.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">如果AppStorage中的属性已经没有订阅者则删除成功，返回true；如果当前仍有订阅者，返回false。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Link<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="linkdeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static Link(propName: string): any</p>     <p>与<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中对应的propName建立双向数据绑定。如果给定的propName在AppStorage中存在，返回与AppStorage中propName对应属性的双向绑定数据。</p>     <p>双向绑定数据的修改会同步回AppStorage中，AppStorage会将变化同步到所有绑定该propName的数据和自定义组件中。</p>     <p>如果AppStorage中不存在propName，则返回undefined。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 7开始支持，从API version 10开始废弃，推荐使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#link10">link</a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AppStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">any</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回双向绑定的数据，如果AppStorage中不存在对应的propName，则返回undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">SetAndLink<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setandlinkdeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static SetAndLink&lt;T&gt;(propName: string, defaultValue: T): SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</p>     <p>与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#linkdeprecated">Link</a>接口类似，如果给定的propName在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中存在，则返回该propName对应的属性的双向绑定数据。如果不存在，则使用defaultValue在AppStorage中创建和初始化propName对应的属性，并返回其双向绑定数据。defaultValue必须为T类型，且不能为null或undefined。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 7开始支持，从API version 10开始废弃，推荐使用<a active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="propdeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1082px;">     <h3 id="setandpropdeprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">SetAndProp<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setandpropdeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static SetAndProp&lt;S&gt;(propName: string, defaultValue: S): SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;S&gt;</p>     <p>与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#propdeprecated">Prop</a>接口类似。如果给定的propName在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中存在，则返回该propName对应的属性的单向绑定数据。如果不存在，则使用defaultValue在AppStorage中创建和初始化propName对应的属性，返回其单向绑定数据。defaultValue必须为S类型，且不能为null或undefined。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 7开始支持，从API version 10开始废弃，推荐使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#setandprop10">setAndProp</a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p> width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AppStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">defaultValue</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">S</td>         <td target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中设置propName对应属性的值，如果newValue的值和propName对应属性的值相同，即不需要做赋值操作，状态变量不会通知UI刷新propName对应属性的值，从API version 12开始，newValue可以为null或undefined。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 815px;">     <h3 id="setorcreatedeprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">SetOrCreate<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setorcreatedeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static SetOrCreate&lt;T&gt;(propName: string, newValue: T): void</p>     <p>如果propName已经在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中存在，则设置propName对应的属性值为newValue。如果不存在，则创建propName属性，值为newValue。</p>     <p>newValue不能为null或undefined。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 7开始支持，从API version 10开始废弃，推荐使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#setorcreate10">setOrCreate</a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.8.1.5.1.4"    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1181px;">     <h3 id="deletedeprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Delete<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="deletedeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static Delete(propName: string): boolean</p>     <p>在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中删除propName对应的属性。</p>     <p>在AppStorage中删除该属性的前提是必须保证该属性没有订阅者。如果有订阅者，则返回false。如果没有订阅者则删除成功并返回true。</p>     <p>属性的订阅者为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#linkdeprecated">Link</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#propdeprecated">Prop</a>等接口绑定的propName，以及<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#storagelink" target="_blank">@StorageLink('propName')</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage#storageprop" target="_blank">@StorageProp('propName')</a>。如果自定义组件中使用@StorageLink('propName')和@StorageProp('propName')或者SubscribedAbstractProperty实例依旧对propName有同步关系，则该属性不能从AppStorage中删除。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 7开始支持，从API version 10开始废弃，推荐使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#delete10">delete</a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AppStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">如果AppStorage中有对应的属性，且该属性已经没有订阅者，则删除成功，返回true。如果属性不存在，或者该属性还存在订阅者，则返回false。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 814px;">     <h3 id="cleardeprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Clear<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="cleardeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static Clear(): boolean</p>     <p>删除<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中所有属性。删除所有属性的前提是，AppStorage已经没有任何订阅者。如果有订阅者，Clear将不会生效并返回false。如果没有订阅者且删除成功则返回true。</p>     <p>订阅者的含义参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#delete10">delete</a>。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 9开始支持，从API version 10开始废弃，推荐使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#clear10">clear</a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">如果AppStorage中的属性已经没有订阅者则删除成功，返回true。否则返回false。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div width="25%">用initializingProperties包含的属性和数值初始化LocalStorage。initializingProperties不能为undefined。默认值为空对象，即初始化时不在LocalStorage中新增属性。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1154px;">     <h3 id="set9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">set<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="set9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>set&lt;T&gt;(propName: string, newValue: T): boolean</p>     <p>在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage" target="_blank">LocalStorage</a>中设置propName对应属性的值。如果newValue的值和propName对应属性的值相同，即不需要做赋值操作，状态变量不会通知UI刷新propName对应属性的值。从API version 12开始，newValue可以为null或undefined。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始，LocalStorage支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰map类型变量" target="_blank">Map</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰set类型变量" target="_blank">Set</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰date类型变量" target="_blank">Date类型</a>，支持null、undefined以及<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#localstorage支持联合类型" target="_blank">联合类型</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">LocalStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">newValue</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">T</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">属性值，从API version 12开始可以为undefined或者null。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">如果LocalStorage中不存在propName对应的属性，返回false。设置成功返回true。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">para</span>: <span class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1298px;">     <h3 id="setorcreate9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setOrCreate<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setorcreate9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setOrCreate&lt;T&gt;(propName: string, newValue: T): boolean</p>     <p>如果propName已经在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage" target="_blank">LocalStorage</a>中存在，并且newValue和propName对应属性的值不同，则设置propName对应属性的值为newValue，否则状态变量不会通知UI刷新propName对应属性的值。</p>     <p>如果propName不存在，则创建propName属性，值为newValue。setOrCreate只可以创建单个LocalStorage的键值对，如果想创建多个LocalStorage键值对，可以多次调用此方法。从API version 12开始，newValue可以为null或undefined。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始，LocalStorage支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰map类型变量" target="_blank">Map</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰set类型变量" target="_blank">Set</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰date类型变量" target="_blank">Date类型</a>，支持null、undefined以及<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#localstorage支持联合类型" target="_blank">联合类型</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.10.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">LocalStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">newValue</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">T</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">属性值，从API version 12开始可以为undefined或者null。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>如果LocalStorage中存在propName，则更新其值为newValue，返回true。</p>          <p>如果LocalStorage中不存在propName，则创建propName，并初始化其值为newValue，返回true。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">ref<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="ref12-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>ref&lt;T&gt;(propName: string): AbstractProperty&lt;T&gt; | undefined</p>     <p>如果给定的propName在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage" target="_blank">LocalStorage</a>中存在，则返回LocalStorage中propName对应属性的引用。否则，返回undefined。</p>     <p>与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#link9">link</a>的功能基本一致，但不需要手动释放返回的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#abstractproperty12">AbstractProperty</a>类型的变量。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">LocalStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#abstractproperty12">AbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</a> | undefined</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">LocalStorage中propName对应属性的引用，如果LocalStorage中不存在对应的propName，则返回undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1274px;">     <h3 id="setandref12-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setAndRef<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setandref12-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setAndRef&lt;T&gt;(propName: string, defaultValue: T): AbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</p>     <p>与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#ref12-1">ref</a>接口类似，如果给定的propName在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage" target="_blank">LocalStorage</a>中存在，则返回LocalStorage中propName对应属性的引用。如果不存在，则使用defaultValue在LocalStorage中创建和初始化propName对应的属性，并返回其引用。defaultValue须为T类型，可以为null或undefined。</p>     <p>与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#setandlink9">setAndLink</a>的功能基本一致，但不需要手动释放返回的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#abstractproperty12">AbstractProperty</a>类型的变量。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始，LocalStorage支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰map类型变量" target="_blank">Map</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰set类型变量" target="_blank">Set</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰date类型变量" target="_blank">Date类型</a>，支持null、undefined以及<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#localstorage支持联合类型" target="_blank">联合类型</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">LocalStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">defaultValue</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">T</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">当propName在LocalStorage中不存在时，使用defaultValue在LocalStorage中初始化propName对应属性的值，defaultValue可以为null或undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#abstractproperty12">AbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">AbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;的实例，为LocalStorage中propName对应属性的引用。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">para</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Record</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>, <span device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">link<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="link9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>link&lt;T&gt;(propName: string): SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</p>     <p>如果给定的propName在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage" target="_blank">LocalStorage</a>实例中存在，则返回与LocalStorage中propName对应属性的双向绑定数据。</p>     <p>双向绑定数据的修改会被同步回LocalStorage中，LocalStorage会将变化同步到所有绑定该propName的数据和Component中。</p>     <p>如果LocalStorage中不存在propName，则返回undefined。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.10.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.10.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">LocalStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#subscribedabstractproperty">SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;的实例，与LocalStorage中propName对应属性的双向绑定的数据，如果LocalStorage中不存在对应的propName，则返回undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">para</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Record</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt; = { <span class="hljs-string">'PropA'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">47</span> };</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">storage</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">LocalStorage</span> = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">LocalStorage</span>(para);</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">linkToPropA1</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">SubscribedAbstractProperty</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt; = storage.<span class="hljs-title function_">link</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'PropA'</span>);</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">linkToPropA2</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">SubscribedAbstractProperty</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt; = storage.<span class="hljs-title function_">link</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'PropA'</span>); <span linkToPropA1.get() == linkToPropA2.get() == 48</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1298px;">     <h3 id="setandlink9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setAndLink<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setandlink9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setAndLink&lt;T&gt;(propName: string, defaultValue: T): SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;T&gt;</p>     <p>与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#link9">link</a>接口类似，如果给定的propName在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage" target="_blank">LocalStorage</a>中存在，则返回该propName对应的属性的双向绑定数据。如果不存在，则使用defaultValue在LocalStorage中创建和初始化propName对应的属性，返回其双向绑定数据。defaultValue必须为T类型，从API version 12开始defaultValue可以为null或undefined。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始，LocalStorage支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰map类型变量" target="_blank">Map</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰set类型变量" target="_blank">Set</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰date类型变量" target="_blank">Date类型</a>，支持null、undefined以及<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#localstorage支持联合类型" target="_blank">联合类型</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">LocalStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">defaultValue</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">T</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">当propName在LocalStorage中不存在时，使用defaultValue在LocalStorage中初始化propName对应属性的值，从API version 12开始defaultValue可以为null或undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">prop<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1274px;">     <h3 id="setandprop9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setAndProp<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setandprop9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setAndProp&lt;S&gt;(propName: string, defaultValue: S): SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;S&gt;</p>     <p>与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#prop9">prop</a>接口类似。如果propName在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage" target="_blank">LocalStorage</a>中存在，则返回该propName对应的属性的单向绑定数据。如果不存在，则使用defaultValue在LocalStorage中创建和初始化propName对应的属性，返回其单向绑定数据。defaultValue必须为S类型，从API version 12开始defaultValue可以为null或undefined。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始，LocalStorage支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰map类型变量" target="_blank">Map</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰set类型变量" target="_blank">Set</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#装饰date类型变量" target="_blank">Date类型</a>，支持null、undefined以及<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#localstorage支持联合类型" target="_blank">联合类型</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">LocalStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">defaultValue</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">S</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">当propName在LocalStorage中不存在，使用defaultValue在LocalStorage中初始化propName对应属性的值，从API version 12开始defaultValue可以为null或undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#subscribedabstractproperty">SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;S&gt;</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">SubscribedAbstractProperty&lt;S&gt;的实例，和LocalStorage中propName对应属性的单向绑定的数据。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106=""
