class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">para</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Record</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>, <span class="hljs-title function_">setAndProp</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'PropB'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">49</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// PropA -&gt; 47, PropB -&gt; 49</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1321px;">     <h3 id="delete9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">delete<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="delete9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>delete(propName: string): boolean</p>     <p>在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage" target="_blank">LocalStorage</a>中删除propName对应的属性。在LocalStorage中删除属性的前提是该属性已经没有订阅者，如果有订阅者，则返回false。如果没有订阅者则删除成功并返回true。</p>     <p>属性的订阅者为：</p>     <ol>      <li>       <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#localstoragelink" target="_blank">@LocalStorageLink</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage#localstorageprop" target="_blank">@LocalStorageProp</a>装饰的变量。</p></li>      <li>       <p>通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#link9">link</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#prop9">prop</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#setandlink9">setAndLink</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#setandprop9">setAndProp</a>接口返回的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#subscribedabstractproperty">SubscribedAbstractProperty</a>的实例。</p></li>     </ol>     <p>如果想要删除这些订阅者，可以通过以下方式：</p>     <ol>      <li>       <p>删除@LocalStorageLink、@LocalStorageProp所在的自定义组件。删除自定义组件请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-page-custom-components-lifecycle#自定义组件的删除" target="_blank">自定义组件的删除</a>。</p></li>      <li>       <p>对link、prop、setAndLink、setAndProp接口返回的SubscribedAbstractProperty的实例调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#abouttobedeleted10">aboutToBeDeleted</a>接口。</p></li>     </ol>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.12.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.12.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.12.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.12.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">propName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">LocalStorage中的属性名。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.14.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.14.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">如果LocalStorage中有对应的属性，且该属性已经没有订阅者，则删除成功，返回true。如果属性不存在，或者该属性还存在订阅者，则返回false。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">clear<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="clear9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>clear(): boolean</p>     <p>删除<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-localstorage" target="_blank">LocalStorage</a>中所有的属性。删除所有属性的前提是已经没有任何订阅者。如果有订阅者，clear不会生效并返回false。如果没有订阅者则删除成功并返回true。</p>     <p>订阅者的含义参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#delete9">delete</a>。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">如果LocalStorage中的属性已经没有任何订阅者，则删除成功，并返回true。否则返回false。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button width="50%">T</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">AppStorage/LocalStorage同步属性的数据。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p> class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1154px;">     <h3 id="set9-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">set<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="set9-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 570px;">     <h2 id="persistpropsoptions10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">PersistPropsOptions<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="persistpropsoptions10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>用于指定持久化属性及其默认值的键值对对象，作为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#persistprops10">persistProps</a>参数传入。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.5.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.5.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.5.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.5.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.5.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">key</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">属性名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">defaultValue</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number | string | boolean | Object</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" 12开始，defaultValue允许为null或undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 274px;">     <h2 id="persistentstorage" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">PersistentStorage<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="persistentstorage" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>PersistentStorage具体UI使用说明，详见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-persiststorage" target="_blank">PersistentStorage(持久化存储UI状态)</a></p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始，PersistentStorage支持null、undefined。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 994px;">     <h3 id="persistprop10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">persistProp<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="persistprop10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static persistProp&lt;T&gt;(key: string, defaultValue: T): void</p>     <p>将<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中key对应的属性持久化到文件中。该接口的调用通常在访问AppStorage之前。</p>     <p>确定属性的类型和值的顺序如下：</p>     <ol>      <li>       <p>如果<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-persiststorage" target="_blank">PersistentStorage</a>文件中存在key对应的属性，在AppStorage中创建对应的propName，并用在PersistentStorage中找到的key的属性初始化。</p></li>      <li>       <p>如果PersistentStorage文件中没有查询到key对应的属性，则在AppStorage中查找key对应的属性。如果找到key对应的属性，则将该属性持久化。</p></li>      <li>       <p>如果AppStorage中也没查找到key对应的属性，则在AppStorage中创建key对应的属性。用defaultValue初始化其值，并将该属性持久化。</p></li>     </ol>     <p>根据上述的初始化流程，如果AppStorage中有该属性，则会使用其值，覆盖掉PersistentStorage文件中的值。由于AppStorage是内存内数据，该行为会导致数据丧失持久化能力。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.63.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.63.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.63.10.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.63.10.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">key</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">属性名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">defaultValue</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">T</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">在PersistentStorage和AppStorage中未查询到时，则使用默认值进行初始化。从API version 12开始允许为null或undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <p>persistProp具体使用，见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-persiststorage#从appstorage中访问persistentstorage初始化的属性" target="_blank">从AppStorage中访问PersistentStorage初始化的属性</a></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 678px;">     <h3 id="deleteprop10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">deleteProp<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="deleteprop10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static deleteProp(key: string): void</p>     <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#persistprop10">persistProp</a>的逆向操作。将key对应的属性从PersistentStorage中删除，后续<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>的操作，对<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-persiststorage" target="_blank">PersistentStorage</a>不会再有影响。该操作会将对应的key从持久化文件中删除，如果希望再次持久化，可以再次调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#persistprop10">persistProp</a>接口。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">PersistProp<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="persistpropdeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static PersistProp&lt;T&gt;(key: string, defaultValue: T): void</p>     <p>将<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中key对应的属性持久化到文件中。该接口的调用通常在访问AppStorage之前。</p>     <p>确定属性的类型和值的顺序如下：</p>     <ol>      <li>       <p>如果<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-persiststorage" target="_blank">PersistentStorage</a>文件中存在key对应的属性，在AppStorage中创建对应的propName，并用在PersistentStorage中找到的key的属性初始化。</p></li>      <li>       <p>如果PersistentStorage文件中没有查询到key对应的属性，则在AppStorage中查找key对应的属性。如果找到key对应的属性，则将该属性持久化。</p></li>      <li>       <p>如果AppStorage也没查找到key对应的属性，则在AppStorage中创建key对应的属性。用defaultValue初始化其值，并将该属性持久化。</p></li>     </ol>     <p>根据上述的初始化流程，如果AppStorage中有该属性，则会使用其值，覆盖掉PersistentStorage文件中的值。由于AppStorage是内存内数据，该行为会导致数据丧失持久化能力。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 10开始废弃，推荐使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#persistprop10">persistProp</a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.67.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.67.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.67.10.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.67.10.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">key</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">属性名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">defaultValue</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">T</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">在PersistentStorage和AppStorage中未查询到时，则使用默认值进行初始化。不允许为null或undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-title class_">PersistentStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title class_">PersistProp</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'highScore'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'0'</span>);</li></ol></pre></div></div> class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static Keys(): Array&lt;string&gt;</p> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">EnvPropsOptions<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="envpropsoptions10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>用于指定环境变量名称及其默认值的键值对对象，作为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#envprops10">envProps</a>参数传入。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.5.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.5.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.5.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.5.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.5.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">key</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">环境变量名称，支持的范围详见<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#内置环境变量说明">内置环境变量说明</a>。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">defaultValue</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number | string | boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">查询不到环境变量key，则使用defaultValue作为默认值存入AppStorage中。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="environment" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Environment<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="environment" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Environment具体使用说明，详见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-environment" target="_blank">Environment(设备环境查询)</a></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1005px;">     <h3 id="envprop10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">envProp<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="envprop10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static envProp&lt;S&gt;(key: string, value: S): boolean</p>     <p>将<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-environment" target="_blank">Environment</a>的内置环境变量key存入<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中。如果系统中未查询到Environment环境变量key的值，则使用默认值value，存入成功，返回true。如果AppStorage中已经有对应的key，则返回false。</p>     <p>所以建议在程序启动的时候调用该接口。</p>     <p>在没有调用envProp的情况下，就使用AppStorage读取环境变量是错误的。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">key</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">环境变量名称，支持的范围详见<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#内置环境变量说明">内置环境变量说明</a>。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">S</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">查询不到环境变量key时，则使用value作为默认值存入AppStorage中。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">如果key对应的属性在AppStorage中存在，则返回false。不存在则在AppStorage中用value作为默认值创建key对应的属性，返回true。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <p>envProp具体使用，详见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-environment#从ui中访问environment参数" target="_blank">从UI中访问Environment参数</a>。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 750px;">     <h3 id="envprops10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">envProps<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="envprops10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static envProps(props: EnvPropsOptions[]): void</p>     <p>和<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#envprop10">envProp</a>类似，不同点在于参数为数组，可以一次性初始化多个数据。建议在应用启动时调用，将系统环境变量批量存入<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">props</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#envpropsoptions10">EnvPropsOptions</a>[]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">系统环境变量和默认值的键值对的数组。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-smf-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">EnvProps<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static EnvProps(props: {key: string; defaultValue: any;}[]): void</p>     <p>和<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#envpropdeprecated">EnvProp</a>类似，不同点在于参数为数组，可以一次性初始化多个数据。建议在应用启动时调用，将系统环境变量批量存入<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-appstorage" target="_blank">AppStorage</a>中。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 10开始废弃，推荐使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-state-management#envprops10">envProps</a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>
